   1: #!/usr/bin/env python3
   2: """Fast fetch cited-content harness (I-deepfix-004 / Fable design 2026-07-09).
   3: 
   4: Proves in ~5 min (parallel) whether the fetch/search module returns the CITED
   5: article for a labeled set of real URLs — replacing the hours-long full-pipeline
   6: loop. It exercises ONE production seam:
   7: 
   8:     ``refetch_for_extraction_with_diagnostics(url, max_chars)`` (live_retriever)
   9: 
  10: which runs the whole chain (``_fetch_content`` -> AccessBypass cascade -> DOI
  11: redirect / ``#page`` anchor / fitz page-slice / Zyte / PDF extractors ->
  12: ``clean_fetch_body`` -> fetch-shell screen -> step-D front-matter screen ->
  13: provenance quote) and returns ``(quote, diagnostics)``.
  14: 
  15: The verdict oracle here is HARNESS-OWNED and INDEPENDENT: it NEVER imports the
  16: production predicate under test (``is_issue_front_matter`` / shell detectors) —
  17: I-wire-013 independence, so a production regression cannot mask itself. The
  18: oracle re-derives front-matter / collision structure from its own rules.
  19: 
  20: Exit codes: 0 green (no FAIL / UNREACHABLE), 1 any FAIL / UNREACHABLE,
  21: 2 VOID (a required fix-flag is OFF or ZYTE_API_KEY is empty — no PASS is ever
  22: written), 3 internal harness error.
  23: 
  24: No mocks: the live network IS the test (§-1.1 — the span text is the proof,
  25: never a count). The only offline part is ``tests/.../test_fetch_harness_oracle.py``,
  26: which unit-tests the oracle functions below against the real banked span heads.
  27: """
  28: from __future__ import annotations
  29: 
  30: import argparse
  31: import json
  32: import os
  33: import re
  34: import sys
  35: import time
  36: import unicodedata
  37: from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, TimeoutError as FutureTimeout
  38: from datetime import datetime, timezone
  39: from pathlib import Path
  40: from typing import Callable, Iterable, Optional
  41: 
  42: import yaml
  43: 
  44: # Make ``src`` importable when run directly (sys.path[0] is scripts/, not root).
  45: _REPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[1]
  46: if str(_REPO_ROOT) not in sys.path:
  47:     sys.path.insert(0, str(_REPO_ROOT))
  48: 
  49: _CASES_PATH = _REPO_ROOT / "config" / "fetch_harness_cases.yaml"
  50: _OUTPUT_ROOT = _REPO_ROOT / "outputs" / "fetch_harness"
  51: 
  52: # ── Verdict labels ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  53: PASS = "PASS"
  54: FAIL = "FAIL"
  55: UNREACHABLE = "UNREACHABLE"
  56: DEGRADED_OK = "DEGRADED_OK"
  57: VOID = "VOID"
  58: 
  59: # ── Oracle tuning (harness-owned; deliberately distinct from production) ─────
  60: ELIGIBLE_MIN_CHARS = 200            # a quote < 200 chars is a refusal, not a span
  61: ORACLE_DOT_LEADER_MIN = 3           # >=3 dot-leader TOC lines => front matter
  62: GOOD_CONTROLS = (
  63:     "good_arxiv_html", "good_feds_note", "good_oa_pdf_nber", "good_oecd_fullreport",
  64: )
  65: # Failure modes that mean "could not reach the source" (block green for `article`).
  66: _UNREACHABLE_MODES = frozenset({"fetch_failed", "timeout", "exception"})
  67: # Failure modes that are an HONEST degrade for `article_or_degrade` /
  68: # `recover_or_disclose` (recover-or-disclose, never a silent wrong span).
  69: _DEGRADE_OK_MODES = frozenset({
  70:     "wrong_content_front_matter", "fetch_shell", "paywall_shell",
  71:     "thin_content", "fetch_failed", "timeout",
  72: })
  73: 
  74: # Dot-leader run (three-or-more dots) then a page number — the canonical TOC line
  75: # shape, robust to space-collapsed single-line PDF extraction. Runs on RAW text
  76: # (squash strips the dots). High precision: never occurs in real article prose.
  77: _ORACLE_DOT_LEADER_RE = re.compile(r"\.{3,}\s*[ivxlcdm\d]{1,5}\b", re.IGNORECASE)
  78: 
  79: 
  80: # ── Oracle primitives (pure; imported by the offline unit tests) ────────────
  81: def squash(text: Optional[str]) -> str:
  82:     """NFKD -> strip combining marks -> casefold -> keep letters+digits only.
  83: 
  84:     Survives PDF hyphen-breaks, diacritics, case, and whitespace. Idempotent, so
  85:     the yaml fingerprints (already squashed) can be squashed again at load time.
  86:     """
  87:     if not text:
  88:         return ""
  89:     nfkd = unicodedata.normalize("NFKD", text)
  90:     no_marks = "".join(ch for ch in nfkd if not unicodedata.combining(ch))
  91:     return "".join(ch for ch in no_marks.casefold() if ch.isalnum())
  92: 
  93: 
  94: def contains_any(squashed_text: str, needles: Iterable[str]) -> bool:
  95:     """True iff ANY squashed needle is a substring. Empty needle-set => True
  96:     (vacuous — ``contains_any-where-listed`` per the design)."""
  97:     needle_list = [n for n in (needles or []) if n]
  98:     if not needle_list:
  99:         return True
 100:     return any(n in squashed_text for n in needle_list)
 101: 
 102: 
 103: def contains_none(squashed_text: str, forbidden: Iterable[str]) -> bool:
 104:     """True iff NO squashed forbidden fingerprint is a substring. Empty => True."""
 105:     return not any(f in squashed_text for f in (forbidden or []) if f)
 106: 
 107: 
 108: def front_matter_structural(quote: Optional[str]) -> bool:
 109:     """INDEPENDENT front-matter detector (does NOT import the production predicate).
 110: 
 111:     Fires on any one high-precision signal:
 112:       1. >= ORACLE_DOT_LEADER_MIN dot-leader-then-page TOC lines (on RAW text).
 113:       2. Cyrillic editorial-board masthead (``редакционная коллегия``).
 114:       3. ``table of contents``.
 115:       4. ``editorial board`` AND an ``issn`` marker co-occur.
 116: 
 117:     Deliberately does NOT fire on a lone ``содержание`` — real poultry-article
 118:     prose ("содержание белка" = protein content) carries that word.
 119:     """
 120:     raw = quote or ""
 121:     if len(_ORACLE_DOT_LEADER_RE.findall(raw)) >= ORACLE_DOT_LEADER_MIN:
 122:         return True
 123:     sq = squash(raw)
 124:     if "редакционнаяколлегия" in sq:
 125:         return True
 126:     if "tableofcontents" in sq:
 127:         return True
 128:     if "editorialboard" in sq and "issn" in sq:
 129:         return True
 130:     return False
 131: 
 132: 
 133: def _work_id(case: dict) -> str:
 134:     """Cited-WORK identity for the collision oracle: DOI when present, else URL."""
 135:     doi = str(case.get("doi") or "").strip().lower()
 136:     if doi:
 137:         return f"doi:{doi}"
 138:     return "url:" + str(case.get("url") or "").strip().lower()
 139: 
 140: 
 141: def identical_span_collision(entries: list[dict]) -> set[str]:
 142:     """Global content-identity collision: group ELIGIBLE entries by squashed span;
 143:     any group whose entries cite >= 2 DIFFERENT works (DOIs/URLs) is a single
 144:     multi-article CONTAINER blob laundered into distinct citations — FAIL them all.
 145: 
 146:     ``entries`` are dicts with keys: name, work_id, squashed_quote, eligible.
 147:     Returns the set of flagged case names.
 148:     """
 149:     by_span: dict[str, list[dict]] = {}
 150:     for e in entries:
 151:         if not e.get("eligible") or not e.get("squashed_quote"):
 152:             continue
 153:         by_span.setdefault(e["squashed_quote"], []).append(e)
 154:     flagged: set[str] = set()
 155:     for group in by_span.values():
 156:         works = {e["work_id"] for e in group}
 157:         if len(works) >= 2:
 158:             flagged.update(e["name"] for e in group)
 159:     return flagged
 160: 
 161: 
 162: def group_distinctness_violations(entries: list[dict]) -> set[str]:
 163:     """Within each declared ``distinct_group``, every ELIGIBLE pair must differ
 164:     after squash. Two same-group entries sharing a squashed span are the same
 165:     laundered blob — flag them. Returns the set of flagged case names."""
 166:     by_group: dict[str, list[dict]] = {}
 167:     for e in entries:
 168:         grp = e.get("group")
 169:         if not grp or not e.get("eligible") or not e.get("squashed_quote"):
 170:             continue
 171:         by_group.setdefault(grp, []).append(e)
 172:     flagged: set[str] = set()
 173:     for members in by_group.values():
 174:         seen: dict[str, str] = {}
 175:         for e in members:
 176:             sq = e["squashed_quote"]
 177:             if sq in seen and seen[sq] != e["name"]:
 178:                 flagged.add(e["name"])
 179:                 flagged.add(seen[sq])
 180:             seen.setdefault(sq, e["name"])
 181:     return flagged
 182: 
 183: 
 184: # ── Per-class verdict ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 185: def verdict_for(expect: str, quote: str, diag: dict, case: dict) -> tuple[str, dict]:
 186:     """Return (verdict, checks). Pure — depends only on the quote/diagnostics and
 187:     the case labels, never on the production predicate."""
 188:     fm = diag.get("failure_mode", "") or ""
 189:     sq = squash(quote)
 190:     eligible = len(quote or "") >= ELIGIBLE_MIN_CHARS
 191:     c_any = contains_any(sq, case.get("contains_squashed") or [])
 192:     c_none = contains_none(sq, case.get("not_contains_squashed") or [])
 193:     fms = front_matter_structural(quote)
 194:     checks = {
 195:         "eligible": eligible, "contains_any": c_any,
 196:         "contains_none": c_none, "front_matter_structural": fms,
 197:     }
 198:     article_pass = (fm == "" and eligible and c_any and c_none and not fms)
 199:     has_positive = bool(case.get("contains_squashed"))
 200: 
 201:     if expect == "article":
 202:         if article_pass:
 203:             return PASS, checks
 204:         if fm in _UNREACHABLE_MODES:
 205:             return UNREACHABLE, checks
 206:         return FAIL, checks
 207: 
 208:     if expect in ("article_or_degrade", "recover_or_disclose"):
 209:         if article_pass:
 210:             return PASS, checks
 211:         if fm in _DEGRADE_OK_MODES:
 212:             return DEGRADED_OK, checks
 213:         return FAIL, checks
 214: 
 215:     if expect == "no_front_matter_span":
 216:         if fm == "wrong_content_front_matter":
 217:             return PASS, checks           # production screen caught it — best case
 218:         if eligible:
 219:             if fms or not c_none:
 220:                 return FAIL, checks       # adopted a cover / TOC / masthead / banned head
 221:             if has_positive and not c_any:
 222:                 return FAIL, checks       # adopted a non-front-matter but wrong-work span
 223:             return PASS, checks           # recovered a real non-front-matter span
 224:         return DEGRADED_OK, checks        # honest refusal — no bad span adopted
 225: 
 226:     if expect == "refused":
 227:         return (FAIL if eligible else PASS), checks
 228: 
 229:     return FAIL, checks                   # unknown expect class => fail loud
 230: 
 231: 
 232: # ── Flag gate (can't fake a pass) ───────────────────────────────────────────
 233: def _falsey(value: Optional[str]) -> bool:
 234:     return (value or "").strip().lower() in ("0", "false", "off", "no", "disabled")
 235: 
 236: 
 237: def check_flags() -> tuple[bool, dict]:
 238:     """Assert every fix-flag is ON and ZYTE_API_KEY is present. Returns
 239:     (ok, flag_states). Any OFF => not ok => the caller writes RESULT VOID."""
 240:     from src.tools.access_bypass import pdf_cited_work_slice_enabled
 241:     from src.polaris_graph.retrieval.shell_detector import (
 242:         cited_span_shell_detect_enabled, span_cited_work_screen_enabled,
 243:     )
 244:     states = {
 245:         "pdf_cited_work_slice_enabled": bool(pdf_cited_work_slice_enabled()),
 246:         "span_cited_work_screen_enabled": bool(span_cited_work_screen_enabled()),
 247:         "cited_span_shell_detect_enabled": bool(cited_span_shell_detect_enabled()),
 248:         "PG_REFETCH_FULL_BODY_on": not _falsey(os.environ.get("PG_REFETCH_FULL_BODY", "1")),
 249:         "PG_DISABLE_ACCESS_BYPASS_off": os.environ.get("PG_DISABLE_ACCESS_BYPASS", "0") != "1",
 250:         "ZYTE_API_KEY_present": bool((os.environ.get("ZYTE_API_KEY") or "").strip()),
 251:     }
 252:     return all(states.values()), states
 253: 
 254: 
 255: def _load_seam() -> Callable[..., tuple[str, dict]]:
 256:     from src.polaris_graph.retrieval.live_retriever import (
 257:         refetch_for_extraction_with_diagnostics,
 258:     )
 259:     return refetch_for_extraction_with_diagnostics
 260: 
 261: 
 262: # ── Case loading ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 263: def load_cases(path: Path = _CASES_PATH) -> list[dict]:
 264:     """Load + normalize the labeled cases. Squashes every fingerprint at load
 265:     (idempotent) so the oracle compares like-for-like."""
 266:     raw = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")) or {}
 267:     cases: list[dict] = []
 268:     for entry in raw.get("cases", []):
 269:         case = dict(entry)
 270:         case["contains_squashed"] = [squash(x) for x in (entry.get("contains") or [])]
 271:         case["not_contains_squashed"] = [squash(x) for x in (entry.get("not_contains") or [])]
 272:         cases.append(case)
 273:     return cases
 274: 
 275: 
 276: def _select(cases: list[dict], only: Optional[list[str]]) -> list[dict]:
 277:     if not only:
 278:         return cases
 279:     wanted = {w.strip() for chunk in only for w in chunk.split(",") if w.strip()}
 280:     sel = [c for c in cases if c.get("name") in wanted or str(c.get("ev") or "") in wanted]
 281:     return sel
 282: 
 283: 
 284: # ── Run one case ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 285: def run_case(case: dict, seam: Callable[..., tuple[str, dict]], quote_max: int) -> dict:
 286:     start = time.monotonic()
 287:     try:
 288:         quote, diag = seam(case["url"], max_chars=quote_max)
 289:     except Exception as exc:               # seam-level exception -> honest failure
 290:         quote, diag = "", {
 291:             "failure_mode": "exception", "exception_type": type(exc).__name__,
 292:             "method": "none", "raw_char_count": 0,
 293:         }
 294:     elapsed = round(time.monotonic() - start, 2)
 295:     verdict, checks = verdict_for(case["expect"], quote, diag, case)
 296:     return {
 297:         "name": case["name"],
 298:         "ev": case.get("ev", ""),
 299:         "url": case["url"],
 300:         "doi": case.get("doi", ""),
 301:         "group": case.get("group", ""),
 302:         "expect": case["expect"],
 303:         "verdict": verdict,
 304:         "failure_mode": diag.get("failure_mode", "") or "",
 305:         "access_method": diag.get("method", "none"),
 306:         "raw_char_count": int(diag.get("raw_char_count", 0) or 0),
 307:         "elapsed_s": elapsed,
 308:         "quote_head": (quote or "")[:300],
 309:         "quote_len": len(quote or ""),
 310:         "checks": checks,
 311:         "work_id": _work_id(case),
 312:         "squashed_quote": squash(quote),
 313:         "eligible": checks["eligible"],
 314:         "collision_reason": "",
 315:     }
 316: 
 317: 
 318: def run_all(cases: list[dict], max_parallel: int, case_timeout: int,
 319:             total_timeout: int, quote_max: int) -> list[dict]:
 320:     seam = _load_seam()
 321:     results: dict[str, dict] = {}
 322:     deadline = time.monotonic() + total_timeout
 323:     with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=max_parallel) as pool:
 324:         futures = {pool.submit(run_case, c, seam, quote_max): c for c in cases}
 325:         for fut, case in futures.items():
 326:             remaining = max(1, min(case_timeout, int(deadline - time.monotonic())))
 327:             try:
 328:                 results[case["name"]] = fut.result(timeout=remaining)
 329:             except FutureTimeout:
 330:                 results[case["name"]] = {
 331:                     "name": case["name"], "ev": case.get("ev", ""), "url": case["url"],
 332:                     "doi": case.get("doi", ""), "group": case.get("group", ""),
 333:                     "expect": case["expect"], "verdict": UNREACHABLE,
 334:                     "failure_mode": "timeout", "access_method": "none",
 335:                     "raw_char_count": 0, "elapsed_s": float(case_timeout),
 336:                     "quote_head": "", "quote_len": 0,
 337:                     "checks": {"eligible": False, "contains_any": False,
 338:                                "contains_none": True, "front_matter_structural": False},
 339:                     "work_id": _work_id(case), "squashed_quote": "",
 340:                     "eligible": False, "collision_reason": "",
 341:                 }
 342:     ordered = [results[c["name"]] for c in cases]
 343:     _apply_collisions(ordered)
 344:     return ordered
 345: 
 346: 
 347: def _apply_collisions(results: list[dict]) -> None:
 348:     """Override to FAIL any case whose eligible span collides across works
 349:     (global) or within its distinct-group. Mutates results in place."""
 350:     flagged = identical_span_collision(results) | group_distinctness_violations(results)
 351:     for r in results:
 352:         if r["name"] in flagged and r["verdict"] in (PASS, DEGRADED_OK):
 353:             r["verdict"] = FAIL
 354:             r["collision_reason"] = "container_collision"
 355: 
 356: 
 357: # ── Reporting ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 358: def _summarize(results: list[dict]) -> dict:
 359:     tally: dict[str, int] = {}
 360:     for r in results:
 361:         tally[r["verdict"]] = tally.get(r["verdict"], 0) + 1
 362:     good_pass = all(
 363:         any(r["name"] == g and r["verdict"] == PASS for r in results)
 364:         for g in GOOD_CONTROLS
 365:     )
 366:     no_fail = not any(r["verdict"] in (FAIL, UNREACHABLE) for r in results)
 367:     return {"tally": tally, "good_controls_all_pass": good_pass, "no_fail": no_fail,
 368:             "authorize_full_pipeline": no_fail and good_pass}
 369: 
 370: 
 371: def write_outputs(results: list[dict], flag_states: dict, run_dir: Path) -> dict:
 372:     run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 373:     summary = _summarize(results)
 374:     payload = {
 375:         "generated_utc": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
 376:         "flag_states": flag_states,
 377:         "summary": summary,
 378:         "cases": results,
 379:     }
 380:     (run_dir / "results.json").write_text(
 381:         json.dumps(payload, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False), encoding="utf-8")
 382: 
 383:     lines = [
 384:         "# Fetch cited-content harness report",
 385:         f"generated_utc: {payload['generated_utc']}",
 386:         "",
 387:         "## Flag states",
 388:     ]
 389:     for k, v in flag_states.items():
 390:         lines.append(f"- {k}: {v}")
 391:     lines += [
 392:         "",
 393:         "## Summary",
 394:         f"- tally: {summary['tally']}",
 395:         f"- all 4 good controls PASS: {summary['good_controls_all_pass']}",
 396:         f"- no FAIL / UNREACHABLE: {summary['no_fail']}",
 397:         f"- AUTHORIZE full pipeline: {summary['authorize_full_pipeline']}",
 398:         "",
 399:         "## Cases",
 400:     ]
 401:     for r in results:
 402:         lines.append(
 403:             f"- [{r['verdict']}] {r['name']} ({r['ev'] or '-'}) expect={r['expect']} "
 404:             f"mode={r['failure_mode'] or 'ok'} via={r['access_method']} "
 405:             f"chars={r['raw_char_count']} {r['elapsed_s']}s"
 406:             + (f" collision={r['collision_reason']}" if r["collision_reason"] else "")
 407:         )
 408:     fails = [r for r in results if r["verdict"] in (FAIL, UNREACHABLE)]
 409:     if fails:
 410:         lines += ["", "## FAIL / UNREACHABLE — offending span heads (first 300 chars)"]
 411:         for r in fails:
 412:             lines.append(f"\n### {r['name']} [{r['verdict']}] mode={r['failure_mode'] or 'ok'}")
 413:             lines.append(f"checks={r['checks']}")
 414:             lines.append(f"span={r['quote_head']!r}")
 415:     (run_dir / "report.md").write_text("\n".join(lines) + "\n", encoding="utf-8")
 416:     return summary
 417: 
 418: 
 419: # ── CLI ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 420: def _build_url_case(url: str, expect: str, contains: Optional[list[str]]) -> dict:
 421:     stems: list[str] = []
 422:     for chunk in (contains or []):
 423:         stems.extend(s for s in chunk.split(",") if s.strip())
 424:     return {
 425:         "name": "adhoc_url", "url": url, "expect": expect,
 426:         "contains": stems, "not_contains": [],
 427:         "contains_squashed": [squash(s) for s in stems], "not_contains_squashed": [],
 428:     }
 429: 
 430: 
 431: def main(argv: Optional[list[str]] = None) -> int:
 432:     ap = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Fetch cited-content harness")
 433:     ap.add_argument("--only", action="append", help="case name(s) or ev id(s), comma-ok")
 434:     ap.add_argument("--rerun-failures", metavar="RESULTS_JSON",
 435:                     help="rerun only FAIL/UNREACHABLE cases from a prior results.json")
 436:     ap.add_argument("--list", action="store_true", help="list cases and exit")
 437:     ap.add_argument("--url", help="ad-hoc single URL (needs --expect)")
 438:     ap.add_argument("--expect", help="expect class for --url")
 439:     ap.add_argument("--contains", action="append", help="fingerprint stem(s) for --url")
 440:     args = ap.parse_args(argv)
 441: 
 442:     try:
 443:         all_cases = load_cases()
 444:     except Exception as exc:               # noqa: BLE001 — surface load errors as exit 3
 445:         print(f"RESULT ERROR - could not load cases: {exc}", file=sys.stderr)
 446:         return 3
 447: 
 448:     if args.list:
 449:         for c in all_cases:
 450:             print(f"{c['name']:<22} {c['expect']:<20} {c.get('ev', '-'):<8} {c['url']}")
 451:         return 0
 452: 
 453:     if args.url:
 454:         if not args.expect:
 455:             print("ERROR: --url requires --expect", file=sys.stderr)
 456:             return 3
 457:         cases = [_build_url_case(args.url, args.expect, args.contains)]
 458:     elif args.rerun_failures:
 459:         try:
 460:             prior = json.loads(Path(args.rerun_failures).read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
 461:         except Exception as exc:           # noqa: BLE001
 462:             print(f"RESULT ERROR - bad --rerun-failures file: {exc}", file=sys.stderr)
 463:             return 3
 464:         fail_names = {c["name"] for c in prior.get("cases", [])
 465:                       if c.get("verdict") in (FAIL, UNREACHABLE)}
 466:         cases = [c for c in all_cases if c["name"] in fail_names]
 467:     else:
 468:         cases = _select(all_cases, args.only)
 469: 
 470:     if not cases:
 471:         print("ERROR: no cases selected", file=sys.stderr)
 472:         return 3
 473: 
 474:     ok, flag_states = check_flags()
 475:     if not ok:
 476:         off = [k for k, v in flag_states.items() if not v]
 477:         print(f"RESULT VOID - FIX FLAGS OFF: {off}", file=sys.stderr)
 478:         return 2
 479: 
 480:     max_parallel = _env_int("PG_HARNESS_MAX_PARALLEL", 12)
 481:     case_timeout = _env_int("PG_HARNESS_CASE_TIMEOUT_S", 240)
 482:     total_timeout = _env_int("PG_HARNESS_TOTAL_TIMEOUT_S", 900)
 483:     quote_max = _env_int("PG_HARNESS_QUOTE_MAX", 2000)
 484: 
 485:     try:
 486:         results = run_all(cases, max_parallel, case_timeout, total_timeout, quote_max)
 487:     except Exception as exc:               # noqa: BLE001 — harness bug, not a data FAIL
 488:         print(f"RESULT ERROR - harness crashed: {exc}", file=sys.stderr)
 489:         return 3
 490: 
 491:     run_dir = _OUTPUT_ROOT / datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime("%Y%m%dT%H%M%SZ")
 492:     summary = write_outputs(results, flag_states, run_dir)
 493: 
 494:     for r in results:
 495:         print(f"[{r['verdict']:<11}] {r['name']:<22} expect={r['expect']:<20} "
 496:               f"mode={r['failure_mode'] or 'ok'}")
 497:     print(f"\ntally={summary['tally']}  good_controls_all_pass="
 498:           f"{summary['good_controls_all_pass']}  "
 499:           f"authorize={summary['authorize_full_pipeline']}")
 500:     print(f"report: {run_dir / 'report.md'}")
 501:     return 0 if summary["no_fail"] else 1
 502: 
 503: 
 504: def _env_int(name: str, default: int) -> int:
 505:     try:
 506:         value = int(os.environ.get(name, default) or default)
 507:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
 508:         return default
 509:     return value if value > 0 else default
 510: 
 511: 
 512: if __name__ == "__main__":
 513:     raise SystemExit(main())

   1: """Offline unit tests for the fetch cited-content harness oracle
   2: (I-deepfix-004 / Fable design 2026-07-09).
   3: 
   4: These are the ONLY offline part of the harness (the live network IS the rest of
   5: the test). They exercise the HARNESS-OWNED oracle — squash / contains / the
   6: INDEPENDENT front_matter_structural detector / the cross-work collision +
   7: distinct-group screens / the per-class verdict — against the REAL banked span
   8: heads named in the design doc. No network, no mocks, no production predicate.
   9: 
  10: The harness is loaded by file path (scripts/ is not a package); its heavy seam
  11: and flag imports are lazy, so importing it here stays offline and cheap.
  12: """
  13: from __future__ import annotations
  14: 
  15: import importlib.util
  16: from pathlib import Path
  17: 
  18: import pytest
  19: 
  20: _HARNESS_PATH = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2] / "scripts" / "fetch_cited_content_harness.py"
  21: _spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location("fetch_cited_content_harness", _HARNESS_PATH)
  22: h = importlib.util.module_from_spec(_spec)
  23: _spec.loader.exec_module(h)
  24: 
  25: 
  26: # ── squash: survives PDF hyphen-breaks, diacritics, case, whitespace ────────
  27: def test_squash_survives_pdf_hyphen_break():
  28:     # A PDF line-wrap hyphenates "generative" and inserts a newline; squash must
  29:     # reunite it so the fingerprint still matches the unbroken title form.
  30:     assert h.squash("Gener-\native AI at Work") == "generativeaiatwork"
  31:     assert h.squash("Generative AI at Work") == "generativeaiatwork"
  32:     assert h.squash("gener-  ative  ai  at  work") == "generativeaiatwork"

 3181: def refetch_for_extraction_with_diagnostics(

 3183: ) -> tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]:

 3078: 
 3079:     Every content-fetch fallback in :func:`_fetch_content` (AccessBypass
 3080:     disabled / unavailable / timed out / raised / produced no result) ends by
 3081:     delegating to :func:`_fetch_content_httpx_naive`. The pre-fix code traced
 3082:     ``fail``/``timeout`` BEFORE that delegation, so a SUCCESSFUL fallback was
 3083:     still recorded as a failure. This helper traces the ACTUAL result instead:
 3084: 
 3085:     * ``status="ok"`` + real ``bytes_received`` (length of fetched content) when
 3086:       the naive fetch returned content,
 3087:     * ``status="fail"`` otherwise — carrying ``primary_reason`` (the reason the
 3088:       primary path fell back, e.g. ``access_bypass_timeout_90s``) in ``error``
 3089:       for diagnostics.
 3090: 
 3091:     ``backend_used="httpx_naive"`` uniformly because the naive fetcher is what
 3092:     actually ran. ``t0`` is the single wall-clock start captured at the top of
 3093:     :func:`_fetch_content` so latency reflects total fetch time. Record-only +
 3094:     fail-safe (``_trace_tool`` swallows its own errors); returns the naive
 3095:     fetcher's tuple unchanged so retrieval behavior is identical to before.
 3096:     """
 3097:     result = _fetch_content_httpx_naive(url, max_chars)
 3098:     content, ok = result[0], result[1]
 3099:     _trace_tool(
 3100:         "fetch_content",
 3101:         target=url,
 3102:         status="ok" if ok else "fail",
 3103:         latency_ms=(time.time() - t0) * 1000.0,
 3104:         backend_used="httpx_naive",
 3105:         bytes_received=len(content) if ok else 0,
 3106:         error="" if ok else str(primary_reason),
 3107:         primary_reason=str(primary_reason),
 3108:     )

 4644:     500-char windows around every decimal found in the full content.
 4645: 
 4646:     Fixes Fix-3: strict_verify was dropping sentences that cited real
 4647:     numbers living outside the first 1500 chars (e.g., STEP 5 -15.2%
 4648:     in the results section of a Nature paper). Caller stores the result
 4649:     as evidence.direct_quote; Phase 4 _find_span_for_decimal will now
 4650:     find the decimal because a window containing it is in the quote.
 4651: 
 4652:     Returns a concatenation: head || "\\n\\n[...]\\n\\n" || window_1 || ...
 4653:     Deduplicates overlapping windows. Caps total length at max_total_chars
 4654:     to keep prompt budget under control.
 4655:     """
 4656:     if not content:
 4657:         return ""
 4658:     # I-wire-013 (#1327) TRUNCATION-AT-SOURCE: repair PDF/HTML line-wrap hyphens
 4659:     # ("patent-\ning" -> "patenting") on the FULL body BEFORE any offset is taken,
 4660:     # so the persisted, cited direct_quote — and every [#ev:id:start-end] offset
 4661:     # the generator later resolves against it — is computed on the de-hyphenated
 4662:     # text. Newlines survive clean_fetch_body (it collapses only [ \t]{2,}), so the
 4663:     # line-wrap break is still present here. Input hygiene only; a legitimate
 4664:     # intra-word hyphen ("co-author", "GLP-1") and multilingual prose are preserved
 4665:     # byte-for-byte. The faithfulness engine (strict_verify / NLI / span-grounding)
 4666:     # is untouched.
 4667:     from src.tools.access_bypass import dehyphenate_line_wraps  # noqa: PLC0415
 4668:     content = dehyphenate_line_wraps(content)
 4669:     if len(content) <= head_chars:
 4670:         return content
 4671:     # I-wire-014 (#1327): snap the head cut back to the last word boundary at/before
 4672:     # ``head_chars`` so the stored span NEVER ends mid-word ("usand workers"). The
 4673:     # integer ``head_chars`` cap below (the ``e > head_chars`` window filter) is
 4674:     # unchanged; only the emitted head STRING is trimmed to a whole word. ``head``
 4675:     # stays a verbatim prefix of the de-hyphenated content (faithfulness-neutral).
 4676:     head = content[:_snap_end_to_word_boundary(content, head_chars)]
 4677: 
 4678:     # Find all decimal positions in the full content
 4679:     positions: list[tuple[int, int]] = []
 4680:     for m in _DECIMAL_PATTERN.finditer(content):
 4681:         start = max(0, m.start() - window_chars // 2)
 4682:         end = min(len(content), m.end() + window_chars // 2)
 4683:         positions.append((start, end))
 4684: 
 4685:     # De-overlap: merge adjacent windows that touch each other
